Source Code

These source-code files were derived from scans of the Colossus 237 (Apollo 8 Command Module) program listing from the private collection of original AGC developer Fred Martin. Scanning was by Ron Burkey. Pre-existing Colossus 249 (Apollo 9 CM) source files were used as a template, and changes between Colossus 249 and Colossus 237 were manually transcribed by a team of volunteers. Note that the page images presented online are of reduced quality, and that additional images are available. Report any conversion errors or legibility problems in page images to info@sandroid.org. Notations on the program listing read, in part:

	GAP: ASSEMBLE REVISION 237 OF AGC PROGRAM COLOSSUS 
	BY NASA 2021111-031  1:17 AUG. 24, 1968
Note that the date is the date of the printout, not the date of the program revision.

012938,000019: 
012939,000020:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME - KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM
012940,000021:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 4      DATE - 27 APRIL 1967      ASSEMBLY - PINDISK REV 17
012941,000022:                                                                                                  #  MOD BY - FILENE
012942,000023:                                                                                                  #  LOG SECTION - PINBALL GAME  BUTTONS AND LIGHTS
012943,000024: 
012944,000025:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION-
012945,000026: 
012946,000027:                                                                                                  #     THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM PROGRAM OPERATES UNDER EXECUTIVE
012947,000028:                                                                                                  #  CONTROL AND PROCESSES INFORMATION EXCHANGED BETWEEN THE AGC AND THE
012948,000029:                                                                                                  #  COMPUTER OPERATOR.  THE INPUTS TO THE PROGRAM ARE FROM THE KEYBOARD,
012949,000030:                                                                                                  #  FROM INTERNAL PROGRAMS, AND FROM THE UPLINK.
012950,000031:                                                                                                  #     THE LANGUAGE OF COMMUNICATION WITH THE PROGRAM IS A PAIR OF WORDS
012951,000032:                                                                                                  #  KNOWN AS VERB AND NOUN.  EACH OF THESE IS REPRESENTED BY A 2 CHARACTER
012952,000033:                                                                                                  #  DECIMAL NUMBER.  THE VERB CODE INDICATES WHAT ACTION IS TO BE TAKEN, THE
012953,000034:                                                                                                  #  NOUN CODE INDICATES TO WHAT THIS ACTION IS APPLIED.  NOUNS USUALLY
012954,000035:                                                                                                  #  REFER TO A GROUP OF ERASABLE REGISTERS.
012955,000036: 
012956,000037:                                                                                                  #  VERBS ARE GROUPED INTO DISPLAYS, LOADS, MONITORS (DISPLAYS THAT ARE
012957,000038:                                                                                                  #  UPDATED ONCE PER SECOND), SPECIAL FUNCTIONS, AND EXTENDED VERBS(THESE
012958,000039:                                                                                                  #  ARE OUTSIDE OF THE DOMAIN OF PINBALL AND CAN BE FOUND UNDER LOG SECTION
012959,000040:                                                                                                  #  :EXTENDED VERBS:).
012960,000041:                                                                                                  #  A LIST OF VERBS AND NOUNS IS GIVEN IN LOG SECTION :ASSEMBLY AND 
012961,000042:                                                                                                  #  OPERATION INFORMATION:.
012962,000043: 
012963,000044: 
012964,000045:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCES-
012965,000046: 
012966,000047:                                                                                                  #  KEYBOARD:
012967,000048:                                                                                                  #     EACH DEPRESSION OF A MAIN (NAVIGATION) KEYBOARD BUTTON ACTIVATES
012968,000049:                                                                                                  #  INTERRUPT KEYRUPT1 (KEYRUPT2) AND PLACES THE 5 BIT KEY CODE INTO 
012969,000050:                                                                                                  #  CHANNEL 15 (CHANNEL 16).  KEYRUPT1 (KEYRUPT2) PLACES THE KEY
012970,000051:                                                                                                  #  CODE INTO MPAC, ENTERS AN EXECUTIVE REQUEST FOR THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY
012971,000052:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM (AT :CHARIN:), AND EXECUTES A RESUME.
012972,000053: 
012973,000054:                                                                                                  #  UPLINK:
012974,000055:                                                                                                  #     EACH WORD RECEIVED BY THE UPLINK ACTIVATES INTERRUPT UPRUPT WHICH
012975,000056:                                                                                                  #  PLACES THE 5 BIT KEY CODE INTO MPAC, ENTERS AN EXECUTIVE REQUEST FOR THE
012976,000057:                                                                                                  #  KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM (AT:CHARIN:) AND EXECUTES A RESUME.
012977,000058: 
012978,000059:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS:
012979,000060:                                                                                                  #     INTERNAL PROGRAMS CALL PINBALL AT :NVSUB: WITH THE DESIRED VERB/NOUN
012980,000061:                                                                                                  #  CODE IN A (LOW 7 BITS FOR NOUN, NEXT 7 BITS FOR VERB).  DETAILS
012981,000062:                                                                                                  #  DESCRIBED ON REMARKS CARDS JUST BEFORE :NVSUB: AND :NVSBWAIT: (SEE
012982,000063:                                                                                                  #  SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBERS).
012983,000064: 
012984,000065: 
012985,000066:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES-
012986,000067: 
012987,000068:                                                                                                  #     IF PINBALL WAS CALLED BY EXTERNAL ACTION, THERE ARE FOUR EXITS:
012988,000069:                                                                                                  #           1) ALL BUT (2), (3), AND (4) EXIT DIRECTLY TO ENDOFJOB.

Page 301 

012990,000071:                                                                                                  #           2) EXTENDED VERBS GO TO THE EXTENDED VERB FAN AS PART OF THE
012991,000072:                                                                                                  #              PINBALL EXECUTIVE JOB WITH PRIORITY 30000.  IT IS THE 
012992,000073:                                                                                                  #              RESPONSIBILITY OF THE EXTENDED VERB CALLED TO EVENTUALLY
012993,000074:                                                                                                  #              CHANGE PRIORITY (IF NECESSARY) AND DO AN ENDOFJOB.
012994,000075:                                                                                                  #              ALSO PINBALL IS A NOVAC JOB. EBANK SET FOR COMMON.
012995,000076:                                                                                                  #           3) VERB 37. CHANGE OF PROGRAM (MAJOR MODE) CALLS :V37: IN THE
012996,000077:                                                                                                  #              SERVICE ROUTINES AS PART OF THE PINBALL EXEC JOB WITH PRIO
012997,000078:                                                                                                  #              30000.  THE NEW PROGRAM CODE (MAJOR MODE) IS LEFT IN A.
012998,000079:                                                                                                  #           4) KEY RELEASE BUTTON CALLS :PINBRNCH: IN THE DISPLAY INTERFACE
012999,000080:                                                                                                  #              ROUTINES AS PART OF THE PINBALL EXEC JOB WITH PRIO 30000 IF 
013000,000081:                                                                                                  #              THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT IS OFF AND :CADRSTOR: IS NOT 40.
013001,000082: 
013002,000083:                                                                                                  #     IF PINBALL WAS CALLED BY INTERNAL PROGRAMS, EXIT FROM PINBALL IS BACK
013003,000084:                                                                                                  #  TO CALLING ROUTINE.  DETAILS DESCRIBED IN REMARKS CARDS JUST BEFORE
013004,000085:                                                                                                  #  :NVSUB: AND :NVSBWAIT: (SEE SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBERS).
013005,000086: 
013006,000087: 
013007,000088:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES-
013008,000089: 
013009,000090:                                                                                                  #  EXTERNAL INITIATION:
013010,000091:                                                                                                  #     IF SOME IMPROPER SEQUENCE OF KEY CODES IS DETECTED, THE OPERATOR
013011,000092:                                                                                                  #  ERROR LIGHT IS TURNED ON AND EXIT IS TO :ENDOFJOB:.
013012,000093: 
013013,000094:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAM INITIATION:
013014,000095:                                                                                                  #     IF AN ILLEGAL V/N COMBINATION IS ATTEMPTED, AN ABORT IS CAUSED
013015,000096:                                                                                                  #  (WITH OCTAL 01501).
013016,000097:                                                                                                  #     IF A SECOND ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO SLEEP IN PINBALL, AN ABORT IS
013017,000098:                                                                                                  #  CAUSED (WITH OCTAL 01206). THERE ARE TWO WAYS TO GO TO SLEEP IN PINBALL:
013018,000099:                                                                                                  #           1) ENDIDLE OR DATAWAIT.
013019,000100:                                                                                                  #           2) NVSBWAIT, PRENVBSY, OR NVSUBUSY.
013020,000101: 
013021,000102:                                                                                                  #  CONDITIONS LEADING TO THE ABOVE ARE DESCRIBED IN FORTHCOMING MIT/IL
013022,000103:                                                                                                  #  E-REPORT DESCRIBING KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY OPERATION FOR 278.
013023,000104: 
013024,000105: 
013025,000106:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT-
013026,000107: 
013027,000108:                                                                                                  #     INFORMATION TO BE SENT TO THE DISPLAY PANEL IS LEFT IN THE :DSPTAB:
013028,000109:                                                                                                  #  BUFFERS REGISTERS (UNDER EXEC CONTROL).  :DSPOUT: (A PART OF T4RUPT)
013029,000110:                                                                                                  #  HANDLES THE PLACING OF THE :DSPTAB: INFORMATION INTO OUTPUT CHANNEL 10
013030,000111:                                                                                                  #  IN INTERRUPT.
013031,000112: 
013032,000113: 
013033,000114:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION-
013034,000115: 
013035,000116:                                                                                                  #     FRESH START AND RESTART INITIALIZE THE NECESSARY E REGISTERS FOR
013036,000117:                                                                                                  #  PINBALL IN :STARTSUB:.  REGISTERS ARE:  DSPTAB BUFFER, CADRSTOR,
013037,000118:                                                                                                  #  REQRET, CLPASS, DSPLOCK, MONSAVE, MONSAVE1, VERBREG, NOUNREG, DSPLIST,
013038,000119:                                                                                                  #  DSPCOUNT, NOUT.
013039,000120:

Page 302 

013041,000122: 
013042,000123:                                                                                                  #  A COMPLETE LIST OF ALL THE ERASABLES (BOTH RESERVED AND TEMPORARIES) FOR
013043,000124:                                                                                                  #  PINBALL IS GIVEN BELOW.
013044,000125: 
013045,000126: 
013046,000127:                                                                                                  #  THE FOLLOWING ARE OF GENERAL INTEREST-
013047,000128: 
013048,000129:                                                                                                  #     REMARKS CARDS PRECEDE THE REFERENCED SYMBOL DEFINITION.  SEE SYMBOL
013049,000130:                                                                                                  #  TABLE TO FIND APPROPRIATE PACE NUMBERS.
013050,000131: 
013051,000132:                                                                                                  #     NVSUB   CALLING POINT FOR INTERNAL USE OF PINBALL.
013052,000133:                                                                                                  #               OF RELATED INTEREST   NVSBWAIT
013053,000134:                                                                                                  #                                     NVSUBUSY
013054,000135:                                                                                                  #                                     PRENVBSY
013055,000136: 
013056,000137:                                                                                                  #     ENDIDLE   ROUTINE FOR INTERNAL PROGRAMS WISHING TO GO TO SLEEP WHILE
013057,000138:                                                                                                  #               AWAITING OPERATORS RESPONSE.
013058,000139: 
013059,000140:                                                                                                  #     DSPMM   ROUTINE BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY DISPLAY A DECIMAL
013060,000141:                                                                                                  #             PROGRAM CODE (MAJOR MODE) IN THE PROGRAM (MAJOR MODE) LIGHTS.
013061,000142:                                                                                                  #             (DSPMM DOES NOT DISPLAY DIRECTLY BUT ENTERS EXEC REQUEST
013062,000143:                                                                                                  #             FOR DSPMMJB WITH PRIO 30000 AND RETURNS TO CALLER.)
013063,000144: 
013064,000145:                                                                                                  #     BLANKSUB   ROUTINE BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY BLANK ANY
013065,000146:                                                                                                  #                COMBINATION OF THE DISPLAY REGISTERS R1, R2, R3.
013066,000147: 
013067,000148:                                                                                                  #     JAMTERM   ROUTINES BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY PERFORM THE
013068,000149:                                                                                                  #     JAMPROC   TERMINATE (V 34) OR PROCEED (V 33) FUNCTION.
013069,000150: 
013070,000151:                                                                                                  #     MONITOR   VERBS FOR PERIODIC ( 1 PER SEC) DISPLAY.
013071,000152: 
013072,000153:                                                                                                  #     PLEASE PERFORM, PLEASE MARK SITUATIONS
013073,000154:                                                                                                  #                  REMARKS DESCRIBING HOW AN INTERNAL ROUTINE SHOULD HANDLE
013074,000155:                                                                                                  #                  THESE SITUATIONS CAN BE FOUND JUST BEFORE :NVSUB: (SEE
013075,000156:                                                                                                  #                  SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBER).
013076,000157: 
013077,000158:                                                                                                  #     THE NOUN TABLE FORMAT IS DESCRIBED ON A PAGE OF REMARKS CARDS JUST
013078,000159:                                                                                                  #     BEFORE :DSPABC: (SEE SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBER).
013079,000160: 
013080,000161:                                                                                                  #     THE NOUN TABLES THEMSELVES ARE FOUND IN LOG SECTION :PINBALL NOUN
013081,000162:                                                                                                  #     TABLES:.
013082,000163: 
013083,000164: 
013084,000165:                                                                                                  #  FOR FURTHER DETAILS ABOUT OPERATION OF THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM
013085,000166:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM, SEE THE MISSION PLAN AND/OR MIT/IL E-2129
013086,000167:                                                                                                  #  DESCRIBING KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY OPERATION FOR 278.
013087,000168: 
013088,000169: 
013089,000170:                                                                                                  #  THE FOLLOWING QUOTATION IS PROVIDED THROUGH THE COURTESY OF THE AUTHORS.
013090,000171: 
013091,000172:                                                                                                  #        ::IT WILL BE PROVED TO THY FACE THAT THOU HAST MEN ABOUT THEE THAT

Page 303 

013093,000174:                                                                                                  #  USUALLY TALK OF A NOUN AND A VERB, AND SUCH ABOMINABLE WORDS AS NO
013094,000175:                                                                                                  #  CHRISTIAN EAR CAN ENDURE TO HEAR.::
013095,000176: 
013096,000177:                                                                                                  #                       HENRY 6, ACT 2, SCENE 4
013097,000178: 
013098,000179: 
013099,000180:                                                                                                  #  THE FOLLOWING ASSIGNMENTS FOR PINBALL ARE MADE ELSEWHERE
013100,000181: 
013101,000182: 
013102,000183:                                                                                                  #  RESERVED FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
013103,000184: 
013104,000185:                                                                                                  #  DSPCOUNT      ERASE                   DISPLAY POSITION INDICATOR
013105,000186:                                                                                                  #  DECBRNCH      ERASE                   +DEC, - DEC, OCT INDICATOR
013106,000187:                                                                                                  #  VERBREG       ERASE                   VERB CODE
013107,000188:                                                                                                  #  NOUNREG       ERASE                   NOUN CODE
013108,000189:                                                                                                  #  XREG          ERASE                   R1 INPUT BUFFER
013109,000190:                                                                                                  #  YREG          ERASE                   R2 INPUT BUFFER
013110,000191:                                                                                                  #  ZREG          ERASE                   R3 INPUT BUFFER
013111,000192:                                                                                                  #  XREGLP        ERASE                   LO PART OF XREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
013112,000193:                                                                                                  #  YREGLP        ERASE                   LO PART OF YREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
013113,000194:                                                                                                  #  HITEMOUT      =       YREGLP          TEMP FOR DISPLAY OF HRS, MIN, SEC
013114,000195:                                                                                                  #                                                 MUST = LOTEMOUT-1.
013115,000196:                                                                                                  #  ZREGLP        ERASE                   LO PART OF ZREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
013116,000197:                                                                                                  #  LOTEMOUT      =       ZREGLP          TEMP FOR DISPLAY OF HRS, MIN, SEC
013117,000198:                                                                                                  #                                                 MUST = HITEMOUT+1.
013118,000199:                                                                                                  #  MODREG        ERASE                   MODE CODE
013119,000200:                                                                                                  #  DSPLOCK       ERASE                   KEYBOARD/SUBROUTINE CALL INTERLOCK
013120,000201:                                                                                                  #  REQRET        ERASE                   RETURN REGISTER FOR LOAD
013121,000202:                                                                                                  #  LOADSTAT      ERASE                   STATUS INDICATOR FOR LOADTST
013122,000203:                                                                                                  #  CLPASS        ERASE                   PASS INDICATOR CLEAR
013123,000204:                                                                                                  #  NOUT          ERASE                   ACTIVITY COUNTER FOR DSPTAB
013124,000205:                                                                                                  #  NOUNCADR      ERASE                   MACHINE CADR FOR NOUN
013125,000206:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE       ERASE                   N/V CODE FOR MONITOR. (= MONSAVE1-1)
013126,000207:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE1      ERASE                   NOUNCADR FOR MONITOR (MATBS) =MONSAVE +1
013127,000208:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE2      ERASE                   NVMONOPT OPTIONS
013128,000209:                                                                                                  #  DSPTAB        ERASE           +13D    0-10,DISPLAY PANEL BUFFER.11-13,C RELAYS
013129,000210:                                                                                                  #  CADRSTOR      ERASE                   ENDIDLE STORAGE
013130,000211:                                                                                                  #  NVQTEM        ERASE                   NVSUB STORAGE FOR CALLING ADDRESS
013131,000212:                                                                                                  #                                        MUST = NVBNKTEM-1
013132,000213:                                                                                                  #  NVBNKTEM      ERASE                   NVSUB STORAGE FOR CALLING BANK
013133,000214:                                                                                                  #                                        MUST = NVQTEM+1
013134,000215:                                                                                                  #  VERBSAVE      ERASE                   NEEDED FOR RECYCLE
013135,000216:                                                                                                  #  DSPLIST       ERASE                   WAITING REG FOR DSP SYST INTERNAL USE
013136,000217:                                                                                                  #  EXTVBACT      REASE                   EXTENDED VERB ACTIVITY INTERLOCK
013137,000218:                                                                                                  #  DSPTEM1       ERASE           +2      BUFFER STORAGE AREA 1 (MOSTLY FOR TIME)
013138,000219:                                                                                                  #  DSPTEM2       ERASE           +2      BUFFER STORAGE AREA 2 (MOSTLY FOR DEG)
013139,000220:                                                                                                  #  END OF ERASABLES RESERVED FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
013140,000221:

013143,000224:

013156,000237:                                                                                                  #  ERCNT         =       POLISH          COUNTER FOR ERROR LIGHT RESET
013157,000238:                                                                                                  #  DECOUNT       =       POLISH          COUNTER FOR SCALING AND DISPLAY (DEC)
013158,000239:

013160,000241:                                                                                                  #  NOUNTEM       =       VBUF            COUNTER FOR MIXNOUN FETCH

013162,000243:                                                                                                  #  DECTEM        =       VBUF            COUNTER FOR FETCH (DEC DISPLAY VERBS)
013163,000244: 
013164,000245:                                                                                                  #  SGNOFF        =       VBUF    +1      TEMP FOR +,- ON
013165,000246:                                                                                                  #  NVTEMP        =       VBUF    +1      TEMP FOR NVSUB
013166,000247:                                                                                                  #  SFTEMP1       =       VBUF    +1      STORAGE FOR SF CONST HI PART(=SFTEMP2-1)
013167,000248:                                                                                                  #  HITEMIN       =       VBUF    +1      TEMP FOR LOAD OF HRS, MIN, SEC
013168,000249:                                                                                                  #                                                   MUST = LOTEMIN-1.
013169,000250:                                                                                                  #  CODE          =       VBUF    +2      FOR DSPIN
013170,000251:                                                                                                  #  SFTEMP2       =       VBUF    +2      STORAGE FOR SF CONST LO PART(=SFTEMP1+1)
013171,000252:                                                                                                  #  LOTEMIN       =       VBUF    +2      TEMP FOR LOAD OF HRS, MIN, SEC
013172,000253:                                                                                                  #                                                   MUST = HITEMIN+1.
013173,000254:                                                                                                  #  MIXTEMP       =       VBUF    +3      FOR MIXNOUN DATA
013174,000255:                                                                                                  #  SIGNRET       =       VBUF    +3      RETURN FOR +,- ON
013175,000256:

013177,000258:

013179,000260:

013218,000299: 
013219,000300: 
013220,000301:                                                                                                  #  ADDITIONAL TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
013221,000302: 
013222,000303:                                                                                                  #  MPAC, THRU MPAC +6
013223,000304:                                                                                                  #  BUF, +1, +2
013224,000305:                                                                                                  #  BUF2, +1, +2
013225,000306:                                                                                                  #  MPTEMP
013226,000307:                                                                                                  #  ADDRWD
013227,000308:                                                                                                  #    END OF ADDITIONAL TEMPS FOR PINBALL EXEC ACTION
013228,000309: 
013229,000310: 
013230,000311:                                                                                                  #  RESERVED FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
013231,000312: 
013232,000313:                                                                                                  #  DSPCNT        ERASE                   COUNTER FOR DSPOUT
013233,000314:                                                                                                  #  UPLOCK        ERASE                   BIT1 = UPLINK INTERLOCK (ACTIVATED BY
013234,000315:                                                                                                  #                                                                                  RECEPTION OF A BAD MESSAGE IN UPLINK)
013235,000316:                                                                                                  #  END OF ERASABLES RESERVED FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
013236,000317: 
013237,000318: 
013238,000319:                                                                                                  #  TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
013239,000320: 
013240,000321:                                                                                                  #  KEYTEMP1      =       WAITEXIT        TEMP FOR KEYRUPT, UPRUPT
013241,000322:                                                                                                  #  DSRUPTEM      =       WAITEXIT        TEMP FOR DSPOUT
013242,000323:                                                                                                  #  KEYTEMP2      =       RUPTAGN         TEMP FOR KEYRUPT, UPRUPT
013243,000324:                                                                                                  #  END OF TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
013244,000325:

Page 306 

013246,000327:                                                                                                  #  THE INPUT CODES ASSUMED FOR THE KEYBOARD ARE,
013247,000328:                                                                                                  #  0        10000
013248,000329:                                                                                                  #  1        00001
013249,000330:                                                                                                  #  9        01001
013250,000331:                                                                                                  #  VERB     10001
013251,000332:                                                                                                  #  ERROR RES10010
013252,000333:                                                                                                  #  KEY RLSE 11001
013253,000334:                                                                                                  #  +        11010
013254,000335:                                                                                                  #  -        11011
013255,000336:                                                                                                  #  ENTER    11100
013256,000337:                                                                                                  #  CLEAR    11110
013257,000338:                                                                                                  #  NOUN     11111
013258,000339: 
013259,000340: 
013260,000341:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT FORMAT FOR DISPLAY PANEL. SET OUT0 TO  AAAABCCCCCDDDDD.
013261,000342:                                                                                                  #  A-S SELECT A RELAYWORD. THIS DETERMINES WHICH PAIR OF CHARACTERS ARE
013262,000343:                                                                                                  #  ENERGIZED.
013263,000344:                                                                                                  #  B FOR SPECIAL RELAYS SUCH AS SIGNS ETC.
013264,000345:                                                                                                  #  C-S  5 BIT RELAY CODE FOR LEFT CHAR OF PAIR SELECTED BY RELAYWORD
013265,000346:                                                                                                  #  D-S  5 BIT RELAY CODE FOR RIGHTCHAR OF PAIR SELECTED BY RELAYWORD.
013266,000347: 
013267,000348:                                                                                                  #  THE PANEL APPEARS AS FOLLOWS,
013268,000349:                                                                                                  #  MD1    MD2                         (MAJOR MODE)
013269,000350:                                                                                                  #  VD1    VD2 (VERB)    ND1    ND2    (NOUN)
013270,000351:                                                                                                  #  R1D1   R1D2   R1D3   R1D4   R1D5   (R1)
013271,000352:                                                                                                  #  R2D1   R2D2   R2D3   R2D4   R2D5   (R2)
013272,000353:                                                                                                  #  R3D1   R3D2   R3D3   R3D4   R3D5   (R3)
013273,000354: 
013274,000355:                                                                                                  #  EACH OF THESE IS GIVEN A DSPCOUNT NUMBER FOR USE WITHIN COMPUTATION ONLY
013275,000356:                                                                                                  #  MD1   25     R2D1  11         ALL ARE OCTAL
013276,000357:                                                                                                  #  MD2   24     R2D2  10
013277,000358:                                                                                                  #  VD1   23     R2D3   7
013278,000359:                                                                                                  #  VD2   22     R2D4   6
013279,000360:                                                                                                  #  ND1   21     R2D5   5
013280,000361:                                                                                                  #  ND2   20     R3D1   4
013281,000362:                                                                                                  #  R1D1  16     R3D2   3
013282,000363:                                                                                                  #  R1D2  15     R3D3   2
013283,000364:                                                                                                  #  R1D3  14     R3D4   1
013284,000365:                                                                                                  #  R1D4  13     R3D5   0
013285,000366:                                                                                                  #  R1D5  12
013286,000367: 
013287,000368: 
013288,000369:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS AN 11 REGISTER TABLE (DSPTAB) FOR THE DISPLAY PANEL.
013289,000370: 
013290,000371:                                                                                                  #  DSPTAB RELAYWD       BIT11     BITS 10-6     BITS 5-1
013291,000372:                                                                                                  #  RELADD
013292,000373:                                                                                                  #  10     1011                    MD1  (25)     MD2  (24)
013293,000374:                                                                                                  #  9      1010                    VD1  (23)     VD2  (22)
013294,000375:                                                                                                  #  8      1001                    ND1  (21)     ND2  (20)
013295,000376:                                                                                                  #  7      1000                                  R1D1 (16)

Page 307 

013297,000378:                                                                                                  #  6      0111          +R1       R1D2 (15)     R1D3 (14)
013298,000379:                                                                                                  #  5      0110          -R1       R1D4 (13)     R1D5 (12)
013299,000380:                                                                                                  #  4      0101          +R2       R2D1 (11)     R2D2 (10)
013300,000381:                                                                                                  #  3      0100          -R2       R2D3 (7)      R2D4 (6)
013301,000382:                                                                                                  #  2      0011                    R2D5 (5)      R3D1 (4)
013302,000383:                                                                                                  #  1      0010          +R3       R3D2 (3)      R3D3 (2)
013303,000384:                                                                                                  #  0      0001          -R3       R3D4 (1)      R3D5 (0)
013304,000385:                                                                                                  #         0000   NO RELAYWORD
013305,000386: 
013306,000387: 
013307,000388:                                                                                                  #  THE 5 BIT OUTPUT RELAY CODES ARE:
013308,000389:                                                                                                  #  BLANK      00000
013309,000390:                                                                                                  #  0          10101
013310,000391:                                                                                                  #  1          00011
013311,000392:                                                                                                  #  2          11001
013312,000393:                                                                                                  #  3          11011
013313,000394:                                                                                                  #  4          01111
013314,000395:                                                                                                  #  5          11110
013315,000396:                                                                                                  #  6          11100
013316,000397:                                                                                                  #  7          10011
013317,000398:                                                                                                  #  8          11101
013318,000399:                                                                                                  #  9          11111
013319,000400: 
013320,000401: 
013321,000402:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT BITS USED BY PINBALL:
013322,000403: 
013323,000404:                                                                                                  #             KEY RELEASE LIGHT    - BIT 5 OF CHANNEL 11
013324,000405:                                                                                                  #             VERB/NOUN FLASH      - BIT 6 OF CHANNEL 11
013325,000406:                                                                                                  #             OPERATOR ERROR LIGHT - BIT 7 OF CHANNEL 11

013737,000818:                                                                                                  #  PASSES.

014032,001113:

Page 323 

014034,001115:                                                                                                  #           NOUN   TABLES
014035,001116: 
014036,001117:                                                                                                  #  NOUN CODE L/40, NORMAL NOUN CASE.  NOUN CODE G/E 40, MIXED NOUN CASE.
014037,001118:                                                                                                  #  FOR NORMAL CASE, NNADTAB CONTAINS ONE       ECADR     FOR EACH NOUN.
014038,001119:                                                                                                  #  +0 INDICATES NOUN NOT USED.   - ENTRY INDICATES MACHINE CADR(E OR F) TO
014039,001120:                                                                                                  #  BE SPECIFIED. -1 INDICATES CHANNEL TO BE SPECIFIED. -0 INDICATES AUGMENT
014040,001121:                                                                                                  #  OF LAST MACHINE CADR SUPPLIED.
014041,001122: 
014042,001123:                                                                                                  #  FOR MIXED CASE, NNADTAB CONTAINS ONE INDIRECT ADDRESS(IDADDREL) IN LOW
014043,001124:                                                                                                  #  10 BITS, AND THE COMPONENT CODE NUMBER IN THE HIGH 5 BITS.
014044,001125: 
014045,001126:                                                                                                  #  NNTYPTAB IS A PACKED TABLE OF THE FORM MMMMMNNNNNPPPPP.
014046,001127: 
014047,001128:                                                                                                  #  FOR THE NORMAL CASE, M-S ARE THE COMPONENT CODE NUMBER.
014048,001129:                                                                                                  #                       N-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE CODE NUMBER.
014049,001130:                                                                                                  #                       P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT CODE NUMBER.
014050,001131: 
014051,001132:                                                                                                  #  MIXED CASE,M-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT3 CODE NUMBER     3 COMPONENT CASE
014052,001133:                                                                                                  #             N-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT2 CODE NUMBER
014053,001134:                                                                                                  #             P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER
014054,001135:                                                                                                  #             N-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT2 CODE NUMBER     2 COMPONENT CASE
014055,001136:                                                                                                  #             P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER
014056,001137:                                                                                                  #             P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER      1 COMPONENT CASE
014057,001138: 
014058,001139:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ALSO AN INDIRECT ADDRESS TABLE(IDADDTAB) FOR MIXED CASE ONLY.
014059,001140:                                                                                                  #  EACH ENTRY CONTAINS ONE ECADR.    IDADDREL IS THE RELATIVE ADDRESS OF
014060,001141:                                                                                                  #  THE FIRST OF THESE ENTRIES.
014061,001142:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ONE ENTRY IN THIS TABLE FOR EACH COMPONENT OF A MIXED NOUN
014062,001143:                                                                                                  #  THEY ARE LISTED IN ORDER OF ASCENDING K.
014063,001144: 
014064,001145:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ALSO A SCALE FACTOR ROUTINE NUMBER TABLE( RUTMXTAB ) FOR MIXED
014065,001146:                                                                                                  #  CASE ONLY. THERE IS ONE ENTRY PER MIXED NOUN. THE FORM IS,
014066,001147:                                                                                                  #        QQQQQRRRRRSSSSS
014067,001148:                                                                                                  #  Q-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 3 CODE NUMBER     3 COMPONENT CASE
014068,001149:                                                                                                  #  R-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 2 CODE NUMBER
014069,001150:                                                                                                  #  S-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 1 CODE NUMBER
014070,001151:                                                                                                  #  R-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 2 CODE NUMBER     2 COMPONENT CASE
014071,001152:                                                                                                  #  S-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 1 CODE NUMBER
014072,001153: 
014073,001154: 
014074,001155:                                                                                                  #  IN OCTAL DISPLAY AND LOAD (OCT OR DEC) VERBS, EXCLUDE USE OF VERBS WHOSE
014075,001156:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT NUMBER IS GREATER THAN THE NUMBER OF COMPONENTS IN NOUN.
014076,001157:                                                                                                  #  (ALL MACHINE ADDRESS TO BE SPECIFIED NOUNS ARE 3 COMPONENT.)
014077,001158: 
014078,001159: 
014079,001160:                                                                                                  #  IN MULTI-COMPONENT LOAD VERBS, NO MIXING OF OCTAL AND DECIMAL DATA
014080,001161:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT WORDS IS ALLOWED. ALARM IF VIOLATION.
014081,001162: 
014082,001163:                                                                                                  #  IN DECIMAL LOADS OF DATA, 5 NUMERICAL CHARACTERS MUST BE KEYED IN
014083,001164:                                                                                                  #  BEFORE EACH ENTER. IF NOT, ALARM.
014084,001165:

Page 324 

014086,001167: 
014087,001168:                                                                                                  #           DISPLAY VERBS

015215,002296:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR ALLOWS OTHER KEYBOARD ACTIVITY. IT IS ENDED BY VERB TERMINATE,
015216,002297:                                                                                                  #  VERB PROCEED WITHOUT DATA, VERB RESEQUENCE,
015217,002298:                                                                                                  #  ANOTHER MONITOR, OR ANY NVSUB CALL THAT PASSES THE DSPLOCK (PROVIDED
015218,002299:                                                                                                  #  THAT THE OPERATOR HAS SOMEHOW ALLOWED THE ENDING OF A MONITOR WHICH
015219,002300:                                                                                                  #  HE HAS INITIATED THROUGH THE KEYBOARD).
015220,002301: 
015221,002302:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR ACTION IS SUSPENDED, BUT NOT ENDED, BY ANY KEYBOARD ACTION,
015222,002303:                                                                                                  #  EXCEPT ERROR LIGHT RESET. IT BEGINS AGAIN WHEN KEY RELEASE IS PERFORMED.
015223,002304:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR SAVES THE NOUN AND APPROPRIATE DISPLAY VERB IN MONSAVE. IT SAVES
015224,002305:                                                                                                  #  NOUNCADR IN MONSAVE1, IF NOUN = MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED. BIT 15 OF
015225,002306:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE1 IS THE KILL MONITOR SIGNAL (KILLER BIT). BIT 14 OF MONSAVE1
015226,002307:                                                                                                  #  INDICATES THE CURRENT MONITOR WAS EXTERNALLY INITIATED (EXTERNAL
015227,002308:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR BIT). IT IS TURNED OFF BY RELDSP AND KILMONON.
015228,002309: 
015229,002310:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE INDICATES IF MONITOR IS ON (+=ON, +0=OFF)
015230,002311:                                                                                                  #  IF MONSAVE IS +, MONITOR ENTERS NO REQUEST, BUT TURNS KILLER BIT OFF.
015231,002312:                                                                                                  #  IF MONSAVE IS +0, MONITOR ENTERS REQUEST AND TURNS KILLER BIT OFF.
015232,002313: 
015233,002314:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB (IF EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT IS OFF), VB=PROCEED WITHOUT DATA,
015234,002315:                                                                                                  #  VB=RESEQUENCE, AND VB=TERMINATE TURN KILL MONITOR BIT ON.
015235,002316: 
015236,002317:                                                                                                  #  IF KILLER BIT IS ON, MONREQ ENTERS NO FURTHER REQUESTS, ZEROS MONSAVE
015237,002318:                                                                                                  #  AND MONSAVE1 (TURNING OFF KILLER BIT AND EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT).

015368,002449: 
015369,002450:                                                                                                  #  DSPFMEM IS USED TO DISPLAY (IN OCTAL) ANY FIXED REGISTER.
015370,002451:                                                                                                  #  IT IS USED WITH NOUN = MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED. THE FCADR OF THE 
015371,002452:                                                                                                  #  DESIRED LOCATION IS THEN PUNCHED IN. IT HANDLES F/F ( FCADR 4000-7777)
015372,002453: 
015373,002454:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS L/E 27, THIS IS ENOUGH.
015374,002455: 
015375,002456:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS G/E 30, THE THIRD COMPONENT OF NOUN 26 (PRIO, ADRES, BBCON)
015376,002457:                                                                                                  #  MUST BE PRELOADED WITH THE DESIRED SUPERBANK BITS (BITS 5,6,7).
015377,002458:                                                                                                  #           V23N26 SHOULD BE USED.
015378,002459: 
015379,002460:                                                                                                  #  SUMMARY
015380,002461:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS L/E 27,                          V27N01E(FCADR)E
015381,002462:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS G/E 30,    V23N26E(SUPERBITS)E   V27N01E(FCADR)E
015382,002463: 
015383,002464: 41,3343           34333        DSPFMEM            CAF      R1D1                                  #  IF F/F, DATACALL USES BANK 02 OR 03.
015384,002465: 41,3344           54777                           TS       DSPCOUNT                              
015385,002466: 41,3345           31047                           CA       DSPTEM1    +2                         #  SUPERBANK BITS WERE PRELOADED INTO
015386,002467: 41,3346           54001                           TS       L                                     #  3RD COMPONENT OF NOUN 26.
015387,002468: 41,3347           31017                           CA       NOUNCADR                              #  ORIGINAL FCADR LOADED STILL IN NOUNCADR.
015388,002469: 41,3350           04610                           TC       SUPDACAL                              #  CALL WITH FCADR IN A, SUPERBITS IN L.

015825,002906:                                                                                                  #  END OF LOAD.

Page 360 

015828,002909:                                                                                                  #  KEY RELEASE ROUTINE
015829,002910: 
015830,002911:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE ALWAYS TURNS OFF THE UPACT LIGHT AND ALWAYS CLEARS DSPLOCK.
015831,002912: 
015832,002913:                                                                                                  #  THE HIGHEST PRIORITY FUNCTION OF THE KEY RELEASE BUTTON IS THE
015833,002914:                                                                                                  #  UNSUSPENDING OF A SUSPENDED MONITOR WHICH WAS EXTERNALLY INITIATED.
015834,002915:                                                                                                  #  THIS FUNCTION IS ACCOMPLISHED BY CLEARING DSPLOCK AND TURNING OFF
015835,002916:                                                                                                  #  THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT IF BOTH DSPLIST AND CADRSTOR ARE EMPTY.
015836,002917: 
015837,002918:                                                                                                  #  IF NO SUCH MONITOR EXISTS, THEN RELDSP IS EXECUTED TO CLEAR DSPLOCK
015838,002919:                                                                                                  #  AND THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT (FREEING THE DISPLAY SYSTEM FOR INTERNAL
015839,002920:                                                                                                  #  USE), TURN OFF THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT, AND WAKE UP ANY JOB IN DSPLIST.
015840,002921: 
015841,002922:                                                                                                  #  IN ADDITION IF THERE IS A JOB IN ENDIDLE, THEN CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED
015842,002923:                                                                                                  #  TO PINBRNCH (IN DISPLAY INTERFACE ROUTINE) TO RE-EXECUTE THE SERIES OF
015843,002924:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB CALLS ETC. THAT PRECEDED THE ENDIDLE CALL STILL AWAITING RESPONSE.
015844,002925:                                                                                                  #  THIS FEATURE IS INTENDED FOR USE WHEN THE OPERATOR HAS BEEN REQUESTED TO
015845,002926:                                                                                                  #  RESPOND TO SOME INTERNAL ACTION THAT USED ENDIDLE, BUT HE HAS WRITTEN
015846,002927:                                                                                                  #  OVER THE INFORMATION ON THE DISPLAY PANEL BY SOME DISPLAYS OF HIS OWN
015847,002928:                                                                                                  #  INITIATION WHICH DO NOT SERVE AS RESPONSES. HITTING KEY RLSE WILL
015848,002929:                                                                                                  #  RE-ESTABLISH THE DISPLAYS TO THE STATE THEY WERE IN BEFORE HE OBSCURED
015849,002930:                                                                                                  #  THEM, SO THAT HE CAN SEE THE WAITING REQUEST.  THIS WORKS ONLY FOR
015850,002931:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS THAT USED ENDIDLE THROUGH MARGARETS DISPLAY
015851,002932:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES.
015852,002933: 
015853,002934: 40,3362           44710        VBRELDSP           CS       BIT3                                  
015854,002935: 40,3363           00006                           EXTEND                                         
015855,002936: 40,3364           03011                           WAND     DSALMOUT                              #  TURN OFF UPACT LITE
015856,002937: 40,3365           10115                           CCS      21/22REG                              #  OLD DSPLOCK
015857,002938: 40,3366           34675                           CAF      BIT14                                 
015858,002939: 40,3367           71021                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT (EMB)
015859,002940: 40,3370           10000                           CCS      A                                     
015860,002941: 40,3371           03400                           TC       UNSUSPEN                              #  OLD DSPLOCK AND EMB BOTH 1, UNSUSPEND,
015861,002942: 40,3372           04473        TSTLTS4            TC       RELDSP                                #  NOT UNSUSPENDING EXTERNAL MONITOR,
015862,002943: 40,3373           11042                           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #   RELEASE DISPLAY SYSTEM AND
015863,002944: 40,3374           03376                           TC       +2                                    #   DO RE-ESTABLISH IF CADRSTOR IS FULL.
015864,002945: 40,3375           05112                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              
015865,002946: 40,3376           04574                           TC       POSTJUMP                              
015866,002947: 40,3377           21176                           CADR     PINBRNCH                              
015867,002948: 40,3400           34714        UNSUSPEN           CAF      ZERO                                  #  EXTERNAL MONITOR IS SUSPENDED,
015868,002949: 40,3401           55012                           TS       DSPLOCK                               #   JUST UNSUSPEND IT BY CLEARING DSPLOCK.
015869,002950: 40,3402           11042                           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #   TURN KEY RELEASE LIGHT OFF IF BOTH
015870,002951: 40,3403           05112                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              #   CADRSTOR AND DSPLIST ARE EMPTY.
015871,002952: 40,3404           04516                           TC       RELDSP1                               
015872,002953: 40,3405           05112                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              
015873,002954: 
015874,002955: 40,3406                        ENDRELDS           EQUALS                                         
015875,002956:

Page 361 

015877,002958:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB IS USED FOR SUB ROUTINE CALLS FROM WITHIN COMPUTER. IT CAN BE
015878,002959:                                                                                                  #  USED TO CALL THE COMBINATION OF ANY DISPLAY, LOAD, OR MONITOR VERB
015879,002960:                                                                                                  #  TOGETHER WITH ANY NOUN AVAILABLE TO THE KEYBOARD.
015880,002961:                                                                                                  #  PLACE 0VVVVVVVNNNNNNN INTO A.
015881,002962:                                                                                                  #  V-S ARE THE 7 BIT VERB CODE.  N-S ARE THE 7 BIT NOUN CODE.
015882,002963: 
015883,002964:                                                                                                  #  IF NVSUB IS CALLED WITH THE FOLLOWING NEGATIVE NUMBERS (RATHER THAN THE
015884,002965:                                                                                                  #  VERB-NOUN CODE) IN A, THEN THE DISPLAY IS BLANKED AS FOLLOWS-
015885,002966:                                                                                                  #   -4 FULL BLANK, -3 LEAVE MODE, -2 LEAVE MODE AND VERB, -1 BLANK R-S ONLY
015886,002967: 
015887,002968:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB CAN BE USED WITH MACH CADR TO BE SPEC BY PLACING THE CADR INTO
015888,002969:                                                                                                  #  MPAC+2 BEFORE THE STANDARD NVSUB CALL.
015889,002970: 
015890,002971:                                                                                                  #   NVSUB RETURNS TO 2+ CALLING LOC AFTER PERFORMING TASK, IF DISPLAY
015891,002972:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS AVAILABLE. THE NEW NOUN AND VERB CODES ARE DISPLAYED.
015892,002973:                                                                                                  #  IF V:S =0, THE NEW NOUN CODE IS DISPLAYED ONLY(RETURN WITH NO FURTHER
015893,002974:                                                                                                  #  ACTION). IF N-S =0, THE NEW VERB CODE IS DISPLAYED ONLY(RETURN WITH NO
015894,002975:                                                                                                  #  FURTHER ACTION).
015895,002976: 
015896,002977:                                                                                                  #  IT RETURNS TO 1+ CALLING LOC WITHOUT PERFORMING TASK, IF DISPLAY
015897,002978:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS BLOCKED (NOTHING IS DISPLAYED IN THIS CASE).
015898,002979:                                                                                                  #  IT DOES TC ABORT (WITH OCT 01501) IF IT ENCOUNTERS A DISPLAY PROGRAM
015899,002980:                                                                                                  #  ALARM CONDITION BEFORE RETURN TO CALLER.
015900,002981: 
015901,002982:                                                                                                  #  THE DISPLAY SYSTEM IS BLOCKED BY THE DEPRESSION OF ANY
015902,002983:                                                                                                  #  KEY, EXCEPT ERROR LIGHT RESET
015903,002984:                                                                                                  #  IT IS RELEASED BY THE KEY RELEASE BUTTON, ALL EXTENDED VERBS,
015904,002985:                                                                                                  #  PROCEED WITHOUT DATA, TERMINATE, RESEQUENCE, INITIALIZE EXECUTIVE,
015905,002986:                                                                                                  #  RECALL PART OF RECALTST IF ENDIDLE WAS USED,
015906,002987:                                                                                                  #  VB = REQUEST EXECUTIVE, VB = REQUEST WAITLIST,
015907,002988:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR SET UP.
015908,002989: 
015909,002990:                                                                                                  #  THE DISPLAY SYSTEM IS ALSO BLOCKED BY THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT, WHICH
015910,002991:                                                                                                  #  INDICATES AN EXTERNALLY INITIATED MONITOR IS RUNNING (SEE MONITOR)
015911,002992: 
015912,002993:                                                                                                  #  A NVSUB CALL THAT PASSES DSPLOCK AND THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT ENDS OLD
015913,002994:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR.
015914,002995: 
015915,002996:                                                                                                  #  DSPLOCK IS THE INTERLOCK FOR USE OF KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM WHICH
015916,002997:                                                                                                  #  LOCKS OUT INTERNAL USE WHENEVER THERE IS EXTERNAL KEYBOARD ACTION.
015917,002998: 
015918,002999:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB SHOULD BE USED TWICE IN SUCCESSION FOR :PLEASE PERFORM: SITUATIONS
015919,003000:                                                                                                  #  (SIMILARLY FOR PLEASE MARK). FIRST PLACE THE CODED NUMBER FOR WHAT
015920,003001:                                                                                                  #  ACTION IS DESIRED OF OPERATOR INTO THEREGISTERS REFERRED TO BY THE
015921,003002:                                                                                                  #  :CHECKLIST: NOUN. GO TO NVSUB WITH A DISPLAY VERB AND THE :CHECKLIST:
015922,003003:                                                                                                  #  NOUN. GO TO NVSUB AGAIN WITH THE :PLEASE PERFORM: VERB AND ZEROS IN THE
015923,003004:                                                                                                  #  LOW 7 BITS. THIS :PASTES UP: THE :PLEASE PERFORM: VERB INTO THE VERB
015924,003005:                                                                                                  #  LIGHTS.
015925,003006: 
015926,003007:                                                                                                  #  NVMONOPT IS AN ENTRY SIMILAR TO NVSUB, BUT REQUIRING AN ADDITIONAL

Page 362 

015928,003009:                                                                                                  #  PARAMETER IN L.  IT SHOULD BE USED ONLY WITH A MONITOR VERB-NOUN CODE IN
015929,003010:                                                                                                  #  A. AFTER EACH MONITOR DISPLAY A *PLEASE* VERB WILL BE PASTED IN THE VERB
015930,003011:                                                                                                  #  LIGHTS OR DATA WILL BE BLANKED (OR BOTH) ACCORDING TO THE OPTIONS
015931,003012:                                                                                                  #  SPECIFIED IN L. IF BITS 8-14 OF L ARE OTHER THAN ZERO, THEN THEY WILL 
015932,003013:                                                                                                  #  BE INTERPRETED AS A VERB CODE AND PASTED IN THE VERB LIGHTS. (THIS VERB
015933,003014:                                                                                                  #  CODE SHOULD DESIGNATE ONE OF THE *PLEASE* VERBS.) IF BITS 1-3 OF L ARE
015934,003015:                                                                                                  #  OTHER THAN ZERO, THEN THEY WILL BE USED TO BLANK DATA BY BEING FED TO
015935,003016:                                                                                                  #  BLANKSUB. IF NVMONOPT IS USED WITH A VERB OTHER THAN A MONITOR VERB,
015936,003017:                                                                                                  #  THE PARAMETER IN L HAS NO EFFECT.
015937,003018: 
015938,003019:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB IN FIXED-FIXED PLACES 2+CALLING LOC INTO NVQTEM, TC NVSUBEND INTO
015939,003020:                                                                                                  #  ENTRET. (THIS WILL RESTORE OLD CALLING BANK BITS)
015940,003021: 
015941,003022:    4170                                           SETLOC   ENDALM     +1

015943,003024:    4170                                           COUNT    02/PIN

016056,003137:    4220           34674        KILMONON           CAF      BIT15                                 #     THIS IS THE KILL MONITOR BIT.

016058,003139:                                                                                                  #                                           MONITOR BIT.
016059,003140:    4222           00002                           TC       Q                                     
016060,003141: 
016061,003142: 
016062,003143:                                                                                                  #  LOADSTAT  +0 INACTIVE(WAITING FOR DATA). SET BY NVSUB
016063,003144:                                                                                                  #            +1  PROCEED NO DATA. SET BY SPECIAL VERB
016064,003145:                                                                                                  #           -1 TERMINATE   SET BY SPECIAL VERB
016065,003146:                                                                                                  #           -0    DATA IN      SET BY END OF LOAD ROUTINE
016066,003147:                                                                                                  #              OR RESEQUENCE   SET BY VERB 32
016067,003148: 
016068,003149: 
016069,003150:                                                                                                  #  L  TC ENDIDLE  (FIXED FIXED)
016070,003151:                                                                                                  #  ROUTINES THAT REQUEST LOADS THROUGH NVSUB SHOULD USE ENDIDLE WHILE
016071,003152:                                                                                                  #  WAITING FOR THE DATA TO BE LOADED. ENDIDLE PUTS CURRENT JOB TO SLEEP.
016072,003153:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE CANNOT BE CALLED FROM ERASABLE OR F/F MEMORY,
016073,003154:                                                                                                  #  SINCE JOB SLEEP AND JOBWAKE CAN HANDLE ONLY FIXED BANKS.
016074,003155:                                                                                                  #  RECALTST TESTS LOADSTAT AND WAKES JOB UP TO,
016075,003156:                                                                                                  #  L+1      FOR TERMINATE
016076,003157:                                                                                                  #  L+2      FOR PROCEED WITHOUT DATA
016077,003158:                                                                                                  #  L+3      FOR DATA IN, OR RESEQUENCE
016078,003159:                                                                                                  #  IT DOES NOTHING IF LOADSTAT INDICATES WAITING FOR DATA.
016079,003160:

Page 365 

016081,003162: 
016082,003163:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE ABORTS (WITH CODE 01206) IF A SECOND JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO SLEEP
016083,003164:                                                                                                  #  IN PINBALL. IN PARTICULAR, IF AN ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO ENDIDLE WHEN
016084,003165:                                                                                                  #  1) CADRSTOR NOT= +0. THIS IS THE CASE WHERE THE CAPACITY OF ENDIDLE IS
016085,003166:                                                                                                  #  EXCEEDED. (+-NZ INDICATE A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO ENDIDLE.)
016086,003167:                                                                                                  #  2) DSPLIST NOT= +0. THIS INDICATES A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO
016087,003168:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY.
016088,003169: 
016089,003170:    4223           22002        ENDIDLE            LXCH     Q                                     #  RETURN ADDRESS INTO L.
016090,003171:    4224           04234                           TC       ISCADR+0                              #  ABORT IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0
016091,003172:    4225           04240                           TC       ISLIST+0                              #  ABORT IF DSPLIST NOT= +0
016092,003173:    4226           30001                           CA       L                                     #  DONT SET DSPLOCK TO 1 SO CAN USE
016093,003174:    4227           74747                           MASK     LOW10                                 #  ENDIDLE WITH NVSUB INITIATED MONITOR.
016094,003175:    4230           60004                           AD       FBANK                                 #  SAME STRATEGY FOR CADR AS MAKECADR.
016095,003176:    4231           55042                           TS       CADRSTOR                              
016096,003177:    4232           05070                           TC       JOBSLEEP                              
016097,003178: 
016098,003179:
