Page 373 

016447,003528:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL USE OF KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM
016448,003529: 
016449,003530:                                                                                                  #  USER MUST SCHEDULE CALLS TO NVSUB SO THAT THERE IS NO CONFLICT OF USE OR
016450,003531:                                                                                                  #  CONFUSION TO OPERATOR. THE OLD GRABLOCK (INTERNAL/INTERNAL INTERLOCK)
016451,003532:                                                                                                  #  HAS BEEN REMOVED AND THE INTERNAL USER NO LONGER HAS THE PROTECTION THIS
016452,003533:                                                                                                  #  OFFERED.
016453,003534: 
016454,003535:                                                                                                  #  THERE ARE TWO WAYS A JOB CAN BE PUT TO SLEEP BY THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
016455,003536:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM.    1) BY ENDIDLE
016456,003537:                                                                                                  #              2) BY NVSUBUSY
016457,003538:                                                                                                  #  THE BASIC CONVENTION IS THAT ONLY ONE JOB WILL BE PERMITTED ASLEEP VIA
016458,003539:                                                                                                  #  THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM AT A TIME. IF A JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
016459,003540:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP BY MEANS OF (1) OR (2) AND THERE IS ALREADY A JOB ASLEEP THAT WAS
016460,003541:                                                                                                  #  PUT TO SLEEP BY (1) OR (2), THEN AN ABORT IS CAUSED.
016461,003542: 
016462,003543: 
016463,003544:                                                                                                  #  THE CALLING SEQUENCE FOR NVSUB IS
016464,003545:                                                                                                  #           CAF    V/N
016465,003546:                                                                                                  #  L        TC     NVSUB
016466,003547:                                                                                                  #  L+1      RETURN HERE IF OPERATOR HAS INTERVENED
016467,003548:                                                                                                  #  L+2      RETURN HERE AFTER EXECUTION
016468,003549: 
016469,003550: 
016470,003551:                                                                                                  #        A ROUTINE CALLED  NVSUBUSY IS PROVIDED (USE IS OPTIONAL)  TO PUT
016471,003552:                                                                                                  #  YOUR JOB TO SLEEP UNTIL THE OPERATOR RELEASES THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
016472,003553:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM. NVSUBUSY ALSO TURNS ON THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT.
016473,003554:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY CANNOT BE CALLED FROM ERASABLE OR F/F MEMORY,
016474,003555:                                                                                                  #  SINCE JOBSLEEP AND JOBWAKE CAN HANDLE ONLY FIXED BANKS.
016475,003556: 
016476,003557: 
016477,003558:                                                                                                  #         THE CALLING SEQUENCE IS
016478,003559:                                                                                                  #           CAF    WAKEFCADR
016479,003560:                                                                                                  #           TC     NVSUBUSY
016480,003561: 
016481,003562: 
016482,003563:                                                                                                  #  .
016483,003564: 
016484,003565: 
016485,003566:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY IS INTENDED FOR USE WHEN AN INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS THE OPERATOR
016486,003567:                                                                                                  #  IS USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM (BY HIS OWN INITIATION). IT IS
016487,003568:                                                                                                  #  NOT INTENDED FOR USE WHEN ONE INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS ANOTHER INTERNAL 
016488,003569:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM.
016489,003570: 
016490,003571: 
016491,003572:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY ABORTS (WITH CODE 01206) IF A SECOND JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
016492,003573:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP IN PINBALL. IN PARTICULAR, IF AN ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO NVSUBUSY
016493,003574:                                                                                                  #  WHEN
016494,003575:                                                                                                  #  1) DSPLIST NOT= +0. THIS IS THE CASE WHERE THE CAPACITY OF THE DSPLIST
016495,003576:                                                                                                  #     IS EXCEEDED.
016496,003577:                                                                                                  #  2) CADRSTOR NOT= +0. THIS INDICATES THAT A JOB IS ALREADY USING

Page 374 

016498,003579:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE. (+-NZ INDICATE A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO ENDIDLE.)
016499,003580: 
016500,003581:    4453           44460        PRENVBSY           CS       2K+3                                  #  SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED
016501,003582:    4454           60002                           AD       Q                                     #  BANKS ONLY DESIRING THE FCADR OF(LOC
016502,003583:    4455           60004                           AD       FBANK                                 #  FROM WHICH THE TC PRENVBSY WAS DONE) -2
016503,003584:    4456           04574        NVSUBUSY           TC       POSTJUMP                              #  TO BE ENTERED.
016504,003585:    4457           10550                           CADR     NVSUBSY1                              
016505,003586:    4460           02003        2K+3               OCT      2003                                  
016506,003587: 
016507,003588:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBSY1 MUST BE IN BANK 27 OR LOWER, SO IT WILL PUT CALLER TO SLEEP
016508,003589:                                                                                                  #  WITH HIS PROPER SUPERBITS.
016509,003590: 
016510,003591: 04,2550                                           SETLOC   ENDSPMM    +1                         
016511,003592: 04,2550                                           COUNT    07/PIN                                
016512,003593: 
016513,003594: 04,2550           54001        NVSUBSY1           TS       L                                     
016514,003595: 04,2551           04234                           TC       ISCADR+0                              #  ABORT IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0.
016515,003596: 04,2552           04240                           TC       ISLIST+0                              #  ABORT IF DSPLIST NOT= +0.
016516,003597: 04,2553           04410                           TC       RELDSPON                              
016517,003598: 04,2554           30001                           CA       L                                     
016518,003599: 04,2555           55043                           TS       DSPLIST                               
016519,003600: 04,2556           05070        ENDNVBSY           TC       JOBSLEEP                              
016520,003601: 
016521,003602: 
016522,003603:                                                                                                  #  NVSBWAIT IS A SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED BANKS ONLY. IF
016523,003604:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS NOT BUSY, IT EXECUTES V/N AND RETURNS TO L+1 (L= LOC FROM
016524,003605:                                                                                                  #  WHICH THE TC NVSBWAIT WAS DONE). IF SYSTEM IS BUSY, IT PUTS CALLING JOB
016525,003606:                                                                                                  #  TO SLEEP WITH L-1 GOING INTO LIST FOR EVENTUAL WAKING UP WHEN SYSTEM
016526,003607:                                                                                                  #  IS NOT BUSY.
016527,003608: 
016528,003609:    4461                                           SETLOC   NVSUBUSY   +3                         
016529,003610:    4461                                           COUNT    02/PIN                                
016530,003611: 
016531,003612:    4461           22007        NVSBWAIT           LXCH     7                                     #  ZERO NVMONOPT OPTIONS
016532,003613:    4462           54123                           TS       NVTEMP                                
016533,003614:    4463           34675                           CAF      BIT14                                 
016534,003615:    4464           71021                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT
016535,003616:    4465           61012                           AD       DSPLOCK                               
016536,003617:    4466           10000                           CCS      A                                     
016537,003618:    4467           14471                           TCF      NVSBWT1                               #  BUSY
016538,003619:    4470           14200                           TCF      NVSBCOM                               #  FREE. NVSUB WILL SAVE L+1 FOR RETURN
016539,003620:                                                                                                  #                                          AFTER EXECUTION.
016540,003621:    4471           24002        NVSBWT1            INCR     Q                                     #  L+2. PRENVBSY WILL PUT L-1 INTO LIST AND
016541,003622:    4472           14453                           TCF      PRENVBSY                              #  GO TO SLEEP.
016542,003623: 
016543,003624: 
016544,003625:                                                                                                  #  RELDSP IS USED BY VBPROC, VBTERM, VBRQEXEC, VBRQWAIT, VBRELDSP, EXTENDED
016545,003626:                                                                                                  #  VERB DISPATCHER, VBRESEQ, RECALTST.
016546,003627:                                                                                                  #  RELDSP1 IS USED BY MONITOR SET UP, VBRELDSP.
016547,003628:    4473           56002        RELDSP             XCH      Q                                     #  SET DSPLOCK TO +0, TURN RELDSP LIGHT

Page 375 

016549,003630:    4474           54144                           TS       RELRET                                #  OFF,  SEARCH DSPLIST
016550,003631:    4475           44675                           CS       BIT14                                 
016551,003632:    4476           00004                           INHINT                                         
016552,003633:    4477           71021                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              
016553,003634:    4500           55021                           TS       MONSAVE1                              #  TURN OFF EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT
016554,003635:    4501           11043                           CCS      DSPLIST                               
016555,003636:    4502           04504                           TC       +2                                    
016556,003637:    4503           04507                           TC       RELDSP2                               #  LIST EMPTY
016557,003638:    4504           34714                           CAF      ZERO                                  
016558,003639:    4505           57043                           XCH      DSPLIST                               
016559,003640:    4506           05074                           TC       JOBWAKE                               
016560,003641:    4507           00003        RELDSP2            RELINT

016685,003766:                                                                                                  #  ERROR LIGHT RESET (RSET) TURNS OFF,
016686,003767:                                                                                                  #  UPLINK ACTIVITY, AUTO, HOLD, FREE, OPERATOR ERROR,
016687,003768:                                                                                                  #  PROG ALM, TRACKER FAIL.
016688,003769:                                                                                                  #  LEAVES GIMBAL LOCK AND NO ATT ALONE.
016689,003770:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO ZEROES THE :TEST ALARM: OUT BIT, WHICH TURNS OFF STBY,RESTART.
016690,003771:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO SETS :CAUTION RESET: TO 1.
016691,003772:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO FORCES BIT 12 OF ALL DSPTAB ENTRIES TO 1.
